| Ttḥezzib deg wanwa ara tesɛud d ameddakel-nnek. |
| Ttilin s umata deg Sswis |  Fṛansa ed Biljik daɣ. |
| Ttmagareɣ-d medden si yal ṣṣenf deg uxeddim-iw. |
| Ttmekiɣ-d dima ayen isɛeddaɣ d lehna deg temẓi. |
| Ttmuquleɣ aɣmis n tmeddit mi ara tetteɣ imensi. |
| Ttuɣ ur ssexsiɣ tiliẓri uqbel ad dduɣ ad ḍḍseɣ. |
| Ttuɣalent-d ar wugur yal mara ad yuɣal s axxam. |
| Ttwabẓen ɣef lǧal n urɣam n yidrimen inagduden. |
| Ttwaferneɣ ɣer Usinat deg sin n yigiman ed tam. |
| Ttwafernen ɣer Usinat deg sin n yigiman ed tam. |
| Ttwaɣent kra n tetteffaḥin i yellan deg ukajju. |
| Ttwaliɣ ikayaden la ttakfen axeṣṣar i usselmed. |
| Ttwaliɣ |  a win yufan |  ad tilid deg wusu imir-a. |
| Ttxemmimeɣ ad izmireɣ ad xedmeɣ aya tameddit-a. |
| Ttxil-k |  efk-iyi-d d acu ara cceɣ. Lluẓeɣ aṭas. |
| Ttxil-k |  efk-iyi-d snat n tqerɛunin timecṭuḥin. |
| Ttxil-k |  ma tesɛiḍ kra n yisseqsiyen |  aru-aɣ-d. |
| Ttxil-k |  smekti-iyi-d ad dduɣ s imsujji azekka. |
| Ttxil-m |  ma tesɛiḍ kra n yisseqsiyen |  aru-aɣ-d. |
| Ttxil-wen |  akken kan ara teẓrem izen-a |  rret-d. |
| Ttxil-wen |  aznet-d kra n yiwen ɣer texxamt-inu. |
| Tuder-d ad tecc imekli n tṣebḥit ɣef tis tamet. |
| Tufa-iyi-d ẓleɣ ɣef umeṭraḥ |  ttwaliɣ tilivizyu. |
| Tuɣ armi telha tfirest |  tṛuḥ tekcem-itt twekka. |
| Tuɣ ɛyiɣ mliḥ |  ulamek ara qqqimeɣ akken beddeɣ. |
